<?php
/**
 * Plugin upgrader for version-based migrations.
 *
 * @package AgentWP\Plugin
 */

namespace AgentWP\Plugin;

/**
 * Manages plugin upgrades and version-based migrations.
 *
 * Runs upgrade steps when the installed version differs from the current version.
 * All upgrade steps are idempotent and safe to re-run.
 *
 * Usage:
 * - Call Upgrader::init() early in boot (plugins_loaded hook)
 * - Add new upgrade steps in get_upgrade_steps() when needed
 * - Each step runs only once when upgrading from a lower version
 */

	public function test_multiple_init_calls_idempotent(): void {
		Upgrader::init();
		$after_first = $this->get_static_property( 'has_run' );

		Upgrader::init();
		$after_second = $this->get_static_property( 'has_run' );

		Upgrader::init();
		$after_third = $this->get_static_property( 'has_run' );

		$this->assertTrue( $after_first );
		$this->assertTrue( $after_second );
		$this->assertTrue( $after_third );
	}

	}

	/**
	 * Get memory store TTL in seconds.
	 *
	 * @return int
	 */
	public function getMemoryTtl(): int {
		return max( 60, (int) $this->options->get( self::OPTION_MEMORY_TTL, self::DEFAULT_MEMORY_TTL ) );
	}

	/**
	 * Set memory store TTL in seconds.
	 *
	 * @param int $ttl TTL in seconds.
	 * @return bool
	 */
	public function setMemoryTtl( int $ttl ): bool {
		return $this->options->set( self::OPTION_MEMORY_TTL, max( 60, $ttl ) );
	}

**Considering updating test version references**

The tests referencing step versions 0.1.1 and 0.1.2 might cause confusion since these relate to version ordering rather than actual releases; changing them to more realistic release versions could align with instructions but isn't strictly required.
thinking
**Evaluating upgrade step version handling**

The current upgrade steps align with the version spec and properly skip steps for installed versions equal or greater, so filtering steps by current version isn't required but could be added safely. Next, checking if AGENTWP_VERSION is defined in the test bootstrap to confirm test assumptions about step versions.

	public function test_upgrade_not_needed_when_version_ahead(): void {
		$installed = '99.0.0';
		$current   = Upgrader::get_current_version();

		$needs_upgrade = version_compare( $installed, $current, '<' );

		$this->assertFalse( $needs_upgrade );
	}

- Updated upgrader unit/behavior/migration tests to reflect the 0.2.0 step and pending-step expectations.

How to verify (exact commands)

Risks / follow-ups
- If future releases add new migrations, ensure new step versions match released versions and update tests accordingly.
